   function addPaidLoginTarget(t) {
        try {
            t.push({key: 'paidlogin', value: document.cookie.indexOf('sso') !== -1 ? 'true' : 'false'});
        } catch (e) {
            console.error(`Couldn't get login status for ad targeting!`);
        }

                                    googletag.pubads().refresh([gptAdSlots[slot]]);

                                googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs(true, true);

                                

                                googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

                                googletag.pubads().addEventListener("slotRenderEnded", function (event) {
                                    var slotId = event.slot.getSlotElementId(),
                                        isHalfPageSlot = slotId === "oms_gpt_rectangle",
                                        $slot = jQuery("#" + slotId);

                                    if (event.isEmpty || slotId === "oms_gpt_billboard" && typeof (no_billboard) != "undefined" && no_billboard) {
                                        $slot.closest(".ad").hide();
                                    } else {
                                        $slot.closest(".ad").show();
                                    }

                                    if (isHalfPageSlot) {
                                        /* Slot contains a half page ad */
                                        if ($slot.height() > 350) {
                                            jQuery(".hide-on-halfpage-ad").hide();
                                            jQuery(".show-on-halfpage-ad").show();
                                        }
                                        /* Slot contains no ad or is smaller than a half page ad */
                                        else {
                                            jQuery(".hide-on-halfpage-ad").show();
                                            jQuery(".show-on-halfpage-ad").hide();
                                        }
                                    }
                                });

                                googletag.enableServices();
                                googletag.pubads().setTargeting("bundesland", ["NW"]);

                                var omsFormatValues = [];
                                
                                    omsFormatValues.push("no_intext");
                                
                                googletag.pubads().setTargeting("oms_format", omsFormatValues);
